beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
    if: Mem(BattleDoing)
      ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
        ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
          checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Minigun'
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Drone'
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'GLD_Ultimate2'
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
          stackObject: (STACK1), (NULL)
          findState: s32'Drone', 5, 2, 5
          isObjectActive: (STACK1)
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
          stackObject: (STACK1), (NULL)
          findState: s32'GLD_Ultimate2_target', 5, 2, 5
          isObjectActive: (STACK1)
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
          stackObject: (STACK1), (NULL)
          findState: s32'GLD_Ultimate2_Laser', 5, 2, 5
          isObjectActive: (STACK1)
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal0)
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(5000)
              modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(42)
            endIf: 
            else: 
              modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(14)
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_GLD', 2, 157
  if: Mem(TrainingValue)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(3)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(4)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(5000)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(5)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(10000)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(40)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(99)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(3)

            storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(51)

beginState: s32'HomingJump'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_Dust_HomingJump'
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(250000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(150000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(-180000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(150000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(100000)
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(50)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
        endIf: 
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
          endIf: 
          else: 
            ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'gld205_07', 5
  displayMesh: s32'arm_single', 1
  sprite: s32'gld205_08', 5
  sprite: s32'gld205_09', 5
  sprite: s32'gld205_10', 1
  sprite: s32'gld025_00', 5
  displayMesh: s32'arm_single', 0
  sprite: s32'gld025_01', 5
  sprite: s32'gld025_02', 4
  sprite: s32'gld025_02', 1
  sprite: s32'gld025_03', 2

beginSubroutine: s32'SecurityLv'
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(5000)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
    checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Minigun'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      statsActionName: s32'Minigun_Lv1'
      missionName: s32'Minigun'
    endIf: 
    checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Drone'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      statsActionName: s32'Drone_Lv1'
      missionName: s32'Drone'
    endIf: 
    checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'GLD_Ultimate2'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      statsActionName: s32'GLD_Ultimate2_Lv1'
      missionName: s32'Ultimate2'
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(10000)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(2)
      checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Minigun'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        statsActionName: s32'Minigun_Lv2'
        missionName: s32'Minigun_Lv2'
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Drone'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        statsActionName: s32'Drone_Lv2'
        missionName: s32'Drone_Lv2'
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'GLD_Ultimate2'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        statsActionName: s32'GLD_Ultimate2_Lv2'
        missionName: s32'Ultimate2_Lv2'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(3)
      checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Minigun'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        statsActionName: s32'Minigun_Lv3'
        missionName: s32'Minigun_Lv3'
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Drone'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        statsActionName: s32'Drone_Lv3'
        missionName: s32'Drone_Lv3'
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'GLD_Ultimate2'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        statsActionName: s32'GLD_Ultimate2_Lv3'
        missionName: s32'Ultimate2_Lv3'
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
  endElse: 
  storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
endSubroutine:

  sprite: s32'gld400_07', 4

  upon: (IDLING)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(3)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)

      sendValuesToObject: 2, 4, 2, 47
      createObjectWithArg: s32'GLD_400_bullet_atk', (EX_POINT_F)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(10)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(2)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(20)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(3)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(30)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon:

  characterSfx: s32'SE_BTL_GLD_07'
  sprite: s32'gld400_09', 3
  createObject: s32'GLD_400_Root', (PLAYER)
  sprite: s32'gld400_10', 3
  createObject: s32'GLD_400_Root', (PLAYER)
  sprite: s32'gld400_11', 3
  createObject: s32'GLD_400_Root', (PLAYER)
  callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_screenshake', Val(3), Val(2), Val(0), Val(0)
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'loop'
  beginLabel: s32'end'
